`id`  varchar(255) NOT NULL ,

CREATE TABLE `incidentcases` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `report` varchar(255) default '',
  `incidentdate` date default NULL,
  `incidenttime` varchar(255) default '',
  `description` varchar(1000) default '',
  `attatchment` varchar(2000) default '',
  `resolution` varchar(255) default '',
  `location` varchar(255) default '',
  `product` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdby` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `modifiedby` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `updatedon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL default 'F',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`createdby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`modifiedby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `customercheckinout` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `customer` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `checkintime` datetime default NULL,
  `checkouttime` datetime default NULL,
  `location` varchar(255) default '',
  `checkinby` varchar(40) DEFAULT '',
  `checkoutby` varchar(40) DEFAULT '',
  `company` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`customer`) REFERENCES `customer` (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`checkinby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`checkoutby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

UPDATE in_stockadjustment SET creationdate=IFNULL(UNIX_TIMESTAMP(createdon)*1000,0);

UPDATE in_goodsrequest SET issueddate=IFNULL(UNIX_TIMESTAMP(issuedon)*1000,0);

UPDATE in_goodsrequest SET collecteddate=IFNULL(UNIX_TIMESTAMP(collectedon)*1000,0);

UPDATE in_goodsrequest SET modifieddate=IFNULL(UNIX_TIMESTAMP(modifiedon)*1000,0);
